# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

Perfect! I've completed the analysis of the Apache Kafka consumer group coordinator's state machine. Here's what I found:

## Summary

I've identified all Java source files in apache/kafka (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489) that implement the consumer group coordinator's state machine, including both the classic (legacy) and modern consumer group protocols.

The analysis revealed **two distinct state machine implementations**:

### Classic Consumer Group Protocol
- **States**: EMPTY → PREPARING_REBALANCE → COMPLETING_REBALANCE → STABLE → DEAD
- **Files**: ClassicGroupState.java, ClassicGroup.java, ClassicGroupMember.java
- **Key transitions**:
  - Join phase: Members transition group from EMPTY/STABLE to PREPARING_REBALANCE
  - Sync phase: Transitions from PREPARING_REBALANCE to COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE

### Modern Consumer Group Protocol  
- **States**: EMPTY → ASSIGNING → RECONCILING → STABLE → DEAD
- **Files**: ConsumerGroup.java, ConsumerGroupMember.java, CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java
- **Per-member states**: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS, UNKNOWN
- **Key feature**: Reconciliation engine that tracks member progress through partition assignment

### Core Coordination Logic
- **GroupMetadataManager.java**: Implements classicGroupJoin(), classicGroupSync(), classicGroupHeartbeat(), and consumerGroupHeartbeat()
- **CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java**: Encapsulates the reconciliation engine for modern protocol
- **GroupCoordinatorShard.java** & **GroupCoordinator.java**: Request handling interfaces

The complete findings have been saved to `/workspace/answer.json` with all relevant files, symbols, and a comprehensive narrative explanation.

STABLE: The group is stable with assigned partitions. Members send heartbeats to maintain membership. Transitions back to PREPARING_REBALANCE on member failure, leave, or new join.\\n5. DEAD: Final state before cleanup.\\n\\nThe ClassicGroup class (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/classic/ClassicGroup.java) manages the group state and transitions through the transitionTo() method, which validates state transitions based on validPreviousStates.\\n\\nModern Consumer Group State Machine:\\nThe modern protocol uses a different state machine defined in group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/ConsumerGroup.java (sg-evals/kafka--0753c489). The ConsumerGroupState enum defines:\\n\\n1. EMPTY: No members in the group.\\n2. ASSIGNING: Members have joined and the coordinator is computing target assignment.\\n3. RECONCILING: Members are reconciling to the target assignment (revoking and acquiring partitions).\\n4. STABLE: All members are reconciled with their assignments.\\n5. DEAD: Final cleanup state.\\n\\nThe modern protocol uses a per-member state machine (MemberState in group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/MemberState.java) tracking member reconciliation progress: STABLE, UNREVOKED_PARTITIONS, UNRELEASED_PARTITIONS, and UNKNOWN.\\n\\nCoordination Logic and State Transitions:\\nThe GroupMetadataManager (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/GroupMetadataManager.java) implements the core coordination logic:\\n\\n- classicGroupJoin(): Handles JoinGroup requests for classic groups, triggering transitions from EMPTY/STABLE to PREPARING_REBALANCE\\n- classicGroupSync(): Handles SyncGroup requests, transitioning from COMPLETING_REBALANCE to STABLE\\n- classicGroupHeartbeat(): Manages heartbeats and detects member failures\\n- consumerGroupHeartbeat(): Handles heartbeats for modern consumer groups with reconciliation logic\\n\\nThe CurrentAssignmentBuilder (group-coordinator/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/coordinator/group/modern/consumer/CurrentAssignmentBuilder.java) encapsulates the reconciliation engine for the modern consumer group protocol, determining necessary revocation and acquisition steps to converge members to target assignments.\\n\\nGroupCoordinatorShard and GroupCoordinator provide the request handling interfaces that delegate to GroupMetadataManager for state machine operations.\"\n}\n",
